< Review>
Today was our first visit to this pastry shop. We were fans of the previous patisserie and wanted to make a comparison. When I saw the limited offerings, and the shape of the chocolate almond croissants which were flatter than I had ever seen, I felt dismayed. My husband chose the Mille Feuille and I decided to gamble on the said croissant which we took home.I was so pleasantly surprised that the puff pastry of the Mille Feuille was still flaky, buttery, crunchy, and the Tahiti Vanilla Cream was smooth, flavorful, but not too sweet. My flaky, buttery croissant was an exquisite bite, the bottom was sugar carmelized contrasting to the upper crust and almond paste filling. Was it because I did not have high expectations that these items were so satisfying? I have no answer, but I will return to try their other offerings. For now I am just enjoying my indulgences and thankful that this patisserie is conveniently located.< /Review>

<username>Wook Chung< /username><response>None</response><text>Simply speechless caliber of pastries and bread. This chain started in Palo Alto and now has 3 locations. Redwood City is the latest and they finally have a decent space to sit and enjoy the lovely bread.

The croissant, and pain au chocolat are out of this world. They both are based on layer pastries, and Colette nails this. Crispy on the outside, soft and chewy on the inside. Other pastries based on crispy layers also do really well like Raspberry Cream Cheese.

Now the price. Each bread is typically above $5. Ridiculous pricing for a piece of bread I'd say. But simply speaking, there is no equal in the Bay Area. So I still give it 5 stars.

So happy that there are more locations and longer store hours to enjoy. Will be returning as frequent as possible.< /text></record>

A lovely facility serving Collette's fabulous product. We have been fans of mademoiselle Collette since Debra opened her patisserie in Menlo Park. It's too quality and could compete in Paris. Zeke Tischler</user_name>
<date>1619835335339</date><rate>5<//rate>< review>
Engine light was on in our 10 year old truck. The code was for an evap leak. Turned out to just be a bad sensor that needed replacement. Very fair and competitive price for the work provided. Honest, quick, and communicative.

Update: 4/30/202
My engine light came back on and wouldn't clear from the system so it wouldn't pass smog. Adolfo Auto Care took my car back and worked on it to track the issue down. They replaced the sensor again as well as several valves, and did every diagnostic they could to solve the problem. Unfortunately it seems the issue is a computer error, which means it has to go back to the dealership for a fix, but that isn't Adolfo Auto Care's fault. When I asked for my bill they flat out refused to even let me pay them even though they did several days of hard work and replaced parts. This is a rare and very honest business staffed by good people. I highly recommend their services.</review>

Clean and very attentive. Everyone who works here is happy and friendly. Service with a smile. The fruit is always fresh (they chop everything). Their new paletas have me excited, there are so many flavors, so creamy, so delicious. The cheese paleta is one of my favorite. They have something for everyone.</Review>

Bacon, chicken, caramelized red onions, brie cheese and spinach. Wow. It came super quick, so if you don't feel like waiting, thin crust is the way to go. We had two leftover slices for lunch the next day - even better extra crispy. The tomato sauce is really, really good. I now understand the hype. On a Saturday night, definitely add your name to the online waitlist 30 - 40 mins before you plan to eat.</Review>

Ok... This isn't you typical Round Table... It's Round Table Clubhouse!.. ok.. üëç other than the awesome pizzas,  I've tried out their garlic cheese toast, nice n crispy.
